",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"any"}]," may flow into ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"unknown"}],", including a corresponding nested generic argument, because ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"unknown"}]," still requires narrowing before use.
